class="main-article-content"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><section><h2 class="ref-req-page-title">Transaction: Sale</h2><div class="page-header__picker sdk-picker cf"><div class="language-picker__wrapper"><button class="js-sdk-picker__trigger sdk-picker__button button button--small"><span class="sdk-picker__title" data-testid="current-language-label">Ruby</span><span class="sdk-picker__description">SDK</span><svg class="icon--svg icon--caret sdk-picker__caret" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Caret down</title><path d="M7.41 7.84L12 12.42l4.59-4.58L18 9.25l-6 6-6-6z"></path><path d="M0-.75h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><img class="icon--fallback" src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/braintree/img/fallback/icon--caret.png" alt="fall back icon"/></svg></button><ul class="sdk-picker__list" style="display:none"><li class="sdk-picker__menu-title">Current Braintree Languages</li><li class="sdk-picker__item"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/java/"><span style="cursor:pointer" class="sdk-picker__link">Java</span></a></li><li class="sdk-picker__item"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/dotnet/"><span style="cursor:pointer" class="sdk-picker__link">.NET</span></a></li><li class="sdk-picker__item"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/node/"><span style="cursor:pointer" class="sdk-picker__link">Node.js</span></a></li><li class="sdk-picker__item"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/php/"><span style="cursor:pointer" class="sdk-picker__link">PHP</span></a></li><li class="sdk-picker__item"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/python/"><span style="cursor:pointer" class="sdk-picker__link">Python</span></a></li><li class="sdk-picker__item"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/"><span style="cursor:pointer" class="sdk-picker__link is-active">Ruby</span></a></li></ul></div></div><span>
    See also the </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction"><span>Transaction</span></a><span> response
    object.</span><p class="markdown-p"></p><span> To create a transaction, you must include an
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#amount"><span class="langAttribute">amount</span></a><span> and either a
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#payment_method_nonce"><span class="langAttribute">payment_method_nonce</span></a><span>, a
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#payment_method_token"><span class="langAttribute">payment_method_token</span></a><span>, or a
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#customer_id"><span class="langAttribute">customer_id</span></a><span>. Passing a
    </span><span class="langAttribute">customer_id</span><span> is equivalent to passing the
    </span><span class="langAttribute">payment_method_token</span><span> of the customer's default payment method. </span><p class="markdown-p"></p><span>Braintree
    offers products that manage risk and fraud related to each transaction. These products can only be
    leveraged if there is adequate data to support the capabilities. The required data can be easily
    added during the Braintree SDK or </span><a href="/braintree/graphql/"><span>Graph QL</span></a><span>. integration, and must
    be done prior using risk products. For additional guidance go to
    </span><a href="/braintree/articles/guides/fraud-tools/premium/overview"><span>Premium Fraud Management Tools</span></a><span>. </span><p class="markdown-p"></p><span>The following example creates a transaction using a
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#payment_method_nonce"><span class="langAttribute">payment_method_nonce</span></a><span> from a client and
    instructs that it should be submitted for settlement immediately using
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#options-submit_for_settlement"><span class="langAttribute">options.submit_for_settlement</span></a><span>. You can see more </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#examples"><span>examples</span></a><span>, including
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#using-a-vaulted-payment-method"><span>using a vaulted payment method</span></a><span>, below the parameter
    reference.

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :amount =&gt; &quot;10.00&quot;,
    :payment_method_nonce =&gt; nonce_from_the_client,
    :device_data =&gt; device_data_from_the_client,
    :options =&gt; {
        :submit_for_settlement =&gt; true
    }
)
if result.success? {
    // See result.transaction for details
} else {
    // Handle errors
}</code></pre></div></div>;<h5>Parameters</h5><div class="api-table"><div class="type-decimal api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="amount"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#amount" ariel-label="amount" data-testid=":amount">:amount</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":amount-type">BigDecimal</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":amount-desc"><p>The billing amount of the request. This value must be greater than 0, and must match the currency format of the merchant account. Can only contain numbers and one decimal point (e.g. <code>x.xx</code>). Can&#x27;t be greater than the maximum allowed by the processor. <a href="/braintree/help?issue=TransactionProcessingQuestion">Contact us</a> for your specific limit.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-map api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="billing"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing" ariel-label="billing" data-testid=":billing">:billing</a></code></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":billing-desc"><div><p>Billing address information associated with a specific customer ID.</p><p>AVS rules are not applied when creating a transaction from a Vault record using a <a href="#payment_method_token">payment method token</a>. We still submit the street address and postal code to the processor to run AVS checks.  The transaction response includes <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction#avs_error_response_code">processor AVS response codes</a>.</p></div></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="billing-company"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing-company" ariel-label="company" data-testid=":company">:company</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":company-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":company-desc"><span>Company name. 255 character maximum.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="billing-country_code_alpha2"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing-country_code_alpha2" ariel-label="country_code_alpha2" data-testid=":country_code_alpha2">:country_code_alpha2</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":country_code_alpha2-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":country_code_alpha2-desc"><div><p>The <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_3166-1_alpha-2">ISO 3166-1 alpha-2</a> country code specified in an address. The gateway only accepts <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/countries#list-of-countries">specific alpha-2 values</a>.</p><p>PayPal transactions <em>must</em> use the alpha-2 format. See PayPal&#x27;s <a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/payments/#definition-address">country code documentation</a> for details.</p></div></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="billing-country_code_alpha3"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing-country_code_alpha3" ariel-label="country_code_alpha3" data-testid=":country_code_alpha3">:country_code_alpha3</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":country_code_alpha3-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":country_code_alpha3-desc"><p>The <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_3166-1_alpha-3">ISO 3166-1 alpha-3</a> country code specified in an address. The gateway only accepts <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/countries#list-of-countries">specific alpha-3 values</a>.</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="billing-country_code_numeric"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing-country_code_numeric" ariel-label="country_code_numeric" data-testid=":country_code_numeric">:country_code_numeric</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":country_code_numeric-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":country_code_numeric-desc"><p>The <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_3166-1_numeric">ISO 3166-1 numeric</a> country code specified in an address. The gateway only accepts <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/countries#list-of-countries">specific numeric values</a>.</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="billing-country_name"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing-country_name" ariel-label="country_name" data-testid=":country_name">:country_name</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":country_name-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":country_name-desc"><p>The country name specified in an address. We only accept <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/countries#list-of-countries">specific country names</a>.</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="billing-extended_address"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing-extended_address" ariel-label="extended_address" data-testid=":extended_address">:extended_address</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":extended_address-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":extended_address-desc"><span>The extended address informationsuch as apartment or suite number. 255 character maximum.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="billing-first_name"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing-first_name" ariel-label="first_name" data-testid=":first_name">:first_name</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":first_name-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":first_name-desc"><span>The first name. The first name value must be less than or equal to 255 characters.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-map api-table-row" id="billing-international_phone"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing-international_phone" ariel-label="international_phone" data-testid=":international_phone">:international_phone</a></code></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":international_phone-desc"><span>The phone number that belongs to the address that is structured with country code and national number.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-2 type-string api-table-row" id="billing-international_phone-country_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing-international_phone-country_code" ariel-label="country_code" data-testid=":country_code">:country_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":country_code-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":country_code-desc"><span>Country code of phone number. 1-3 digits. Required.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-2 type-string api-table-row" id="billing-international_phone-national_number"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing-international_phone-national_number" ariel-label="national_number" data-testid=":national_number">:national_number</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":national_number-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":national_number-desc"><span>National number of phone number. 4-12 digits. Required.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="billing-last_name"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing-last_name" ariel-label="last_name" data-testid=":last_name">:last_name</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":last_name-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":last_name-desc"><span>The last name. <p class=" markdown-p"><em>We recommend using <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#payment_method_nonce">payment_method_nonce</a></code> to avoid any PCI concerns with raw credit card data being present on your server.</em></p>
<p class=" markdown-p">A credit or debit payment method.</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="credit_card-cardholder_name"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#credit_card-cardholder_name" ariel-label="cardholder_name" data-testid=":cardholder_name">:cardholder_name</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":cardholder_name-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":cardholder_name-desc"><span>The name associated with the credit card. CVV is not required when creating a transaction from Vault tokens; CVV rules will be applied to transactions if and only if the CVV is supplied with the tokens.</p><p>CVV checking can also be done when you create or update the Vault record by using <a href="/braintree/docs/guides/credit-cards/server-side#card-verification">card verification</a>.</p></div></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="credit_card-expiration_date"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#credit_card-expiration_date" ariel-label="expiration_date" data-testid=":expiration_date">:expiration_date</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":expiration_date-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":expiration_date-desc"><span>The expiration date, formatted <code>MM/YY</code> or <code>MM/YYYY</code>. Querying this value returns a collection of custom field values stored on the transaction object.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-map api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="customer"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#customer" ariel-label="customer" data-testid=":customer">:customer</a></code></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":customer-desc"><p>When <a href="#storing-in-vault">storing a new customer in the Vault</a>, you can use this object to specify the customer&#x27;s details. If you receive a <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/validation-errors/all">validation error</a> of <code>92203</code> or if your dynamic descriptors are not displaying as expected, please <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/help?issue=updateDescriptor">contact us</a>.</em></p>
<p class=" markdown-p">Dynamic descriptors are sent on a per-transaction basis and define what will appear on your customers&#x27; credit card statements for a specific purchase. The clearer the description of your product, the less likely customers will issue chargebacks due to confusion or non-recognition.</p>
<br/>
<p class=" markdown-p"><br/> See the dynamic descriptor <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#dynamic-descriptors">example</a> for additional information.</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="descriptor-name"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#descriptor-name" ariel-label="name" data-testid=":name">:name</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":name-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":name-desc"><p>The value in the business name field of a customer&#x27;s statement. The specific length/character requirements for this value depend on your processor. <a href="/braintree/help?issue=updateDescriptor">Contact us</a> for assistance.</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="descriptor-phone"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#descriptor-phone" ariel-label="phone" data-testid=":phone">:phone</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":phone-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":phone-desc"><span>The value in the phone number field of a customer&#x27;s statement. Phone must be 10-14 characters and can only contain numbers, hyphens and parentheses.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="descriptor-url"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#descriptor-url" ariel-label="url" data-testid=":url">:url</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":url-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":url-desc"><span>The value in the URL/web address field of a customer&#x27;s statement. The URL must be 13 characters or shorter.</span></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="device_data"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#device_data" ariel-label="device_data" data-testid=":device_data">:device_data</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":device_data-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":device_data-desc"><div><p>Customer device information. <strong>Required</strong> in the following cases:</p><ul><li>When using <a href="/braintree/docs/guides/premium-fraud-management-tools/overview">Premium Fraud Management Tools</a></li><li>When creating one-time <a href="/braintree/docs/guides/paypal/vault">Vaulted PayPal transactions</a></li><li>When creating <a href="/braintree/docs/guides/venmo/overview">Venmo transactions</a></li></ul><p>The value can either be a raw PayPal Risk Correlation ID string (also known as the &quot;PayPal Correlation ID&quot; or simply the &quot;Correlation ID&quot;) or a JSON-escaped hash string returned by the Braintree client SDK. When using SDK-provided string, ensure that the whole string is submitted, as it contains multiple key-value pairs. These may include the Device Session ID (a unique identifier for a customer device), a Fraud Merchant ID, and the PayPal Risk Correlation ID.</p></div></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="device_session_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#device_session_id" ariel-label="device_session_id" data-testid=":device_session_id">:device_session_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":device_session_id-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":device_session_id-desc"><p class=" markdown-p"><strong>Deprecated.</strong></p>
<p class=" markdown-p"><em>We recommend including the device session ID  within <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#device_data">device_data</a></code>.</em></p></span></div></div><div class="type-decimal api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="discount_amount"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#discount_amount" ariel-label="discount_amount" data-testid=":discount_amount">:discount_amount</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":discount_amount-type">BigDecimal</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":discount_amount-desc"><p>A <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/level-2-and-3-processing/required-fields#level-3-data">Level 3 field</a> that specifies the discount amount that was included in the total transaction amount. It can&#x27;t be negative, and it does not add to the total transaction amount. This Braintree line-item field is not used by PayPal.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="exchange_rate_quote_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#exchange_rate_quote_id" ariel-label="exchange_rate_quote_id" data-testid=":exchange_rate_quote_id">:exchange_rate_quote_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":exchange_rate_quote_id-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":exchange_rate_quote_id-desc"><span>The ID of a previously generated exchange rate quote to be used for presentment to settlement currency conversion. An ID obtained earlier can be used to get a new quote for the same currency pair and different base amount as long as the ID has not expired.</span></span></div></div><div class="type-map api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="external_vault"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#external_vault" ariel-label="external_vault" data-testid=":external_vault">:external_vault</a></code></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":external_vault-desc"><span>Options used to indicate when a payment method is externally vaulted. These fields should be provided when storing a customer&#x27;s payment methods in an external vault (e.g. third-party vault, not tokenizing through Braintree).</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="external_vault-previous_network_transaction_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#external_vault-previous_network_transaction_id" ariel-label="previous_network_transaction_id" data-testid=":previous_network_transaction_id">:previous_network_transaction_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":previous_network_transaction_id-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":previous_network_transaction_id-desc"><span>Network transaction identifier issued by the card brand networks during a previous transaction. Card brand networks provide network transaction identifiers to improve authorization approval rates for stored credential transactions.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="external_vault-status"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#external_vault-status" ariel-label="status" data-testid=":status">:status</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":status-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":status-desc"><div><p>The option indicates the vaulted status of the externally vaulted payment method. Accepted values:</p><ul><li><code>vaulted</code> = Indicates the payment method is already stored on behalf of the customer.</li><li><code>will_vault</code> = Indicates the payment method is intended to be vaulted upon successful processing of the transaction.</li></ul></div></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="fraud_merchant_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#fraud_merchant_id" ariel-label="fraud_merchant_id" data-testid=":fraud_merchant_id">:fraud_merchant_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":fraud_merchant_id-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":fraud_merchant_id-desc"><span>Deprecated. A unique, numeric identifier for a Kount account. Required only when you have a direct relationship with Kount, including a <code>fraud_merchant_id</code> with your requests ensures that we will route them to your specific Kount account for evaluation.</span></span></div></div><div class="type-map api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="line_items"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#line_items" ariel-label="line_items" data-testid=":line_items">:line_items</a></code></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":line_items-desc"><p>The line items for this transaction. It can include up to 249 line items. If your merchant account has been configured for <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/level-2-and-3-processing/required-fields#level-3-data">Level 3 processing</a> this field will be passed to the processor on your behalf.</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="line_items-commodity_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#line_items-commodity_code" ariel-label="commodity_code" data-testid=":commodity_code">:commodity_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":commodity_code-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":commodity_code-desc"><span>Code used to classify items purchased and track the total amount spent across various categories of products and services. Different corporate purchasing organizations may use different standards, but the <a href="https://www.unspsc.org/">United Nations Standard Products and Services Code (UNSPSC)</a> is frequently used. Maximum 12 characters. This Braintree line-item field is not used by PayPal. For the US Visa CEDP, required for Level 3 interchange.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="line_items-description"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#line_items-description" ariel-label="description" data-testid=":description">:description</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":description-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":description-desc"><span>Item description. Maximum 127 characters.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-decimal api-table-row" id="line_items-discount_amount"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#line_items-discount_amount" ariel-label="discount_amount" data-testid=":discount_amount">:discount_amount</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":discount_amount-type">BigDecimal</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":discount_amount-desc"><span>Discount amount for the line item. Can include up to 2 decimal places. This value can&#x27;t be negative. This Braintree line-item field is not used by PayPal. For the US Visa CEDP, must be provided if discount exists.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="line_items-kind"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#line_items-kind" ariel-label="kind" data-testid=":kind">:kind</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":kind-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":kind-desc"><div><p>Indicates whether the line item is a debit (sale) or credit (refund) to the customer. Accepted values:</p><ul><li><code>&quot;debit&quot;</code></li><li><code>&quot;credit&quot;</code></li></ul></div></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="line_items-name"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#line_items-name" ariel-label="name" data-testid=":name">:name</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":name-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":name-desc"><span>Item name. Maximum 35 characters, or 127 characters for PayPal transactions. For the US Visa CEDP, the item name should reflect the purchased item and must not be the same as the merchant name.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="line_items-product_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#line_items-product_code" ariel-label="product_code" data-testid=":product_code">:product_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":product_code-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":product_code-desc"><span>Product code for the item. For the US Visa CEDP, required for Level 3 interchange.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-decimal api-table-row" id="line_items-quantity"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#line_items-quantity" ariel-label="quantity" data-testid=":quantity">:quantity</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":quantity-type">BigDecimal</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":quantity-desc"><span>Number of units of the item purchased. This value can&#x27;t be negative or zero.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-decimal api-table-row" id="line_items-total_amount"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#line_items-total_amount" ariel-label="total_amount" data-testid=":total_amount">:total_amount</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":total_amount-type">BigDecimal</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":total_amount-desc"><span>Quantity x unit amount. Zero is allowed for PayPal transactions.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="line_items-unit_of_measure"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#line_items-unit_of_measure" ariel-label="unit_of_measure" data-testid=":unit_of_measure">:unit_of_measure</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":unit_of_measure-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":unit_of_measure-desc"><span>The unit of measure or the unit of measure code. If specified, you must also provide the UPC type.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="line_items-upc_type"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#line_items-upc_type" ariel-label="upc_type" data-testid=":upc_type">:upc_type</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":upc_type-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":upc_type-desc"><div><p>UPC type for the item. If no merchant account ID is specified, we will use your default merchant account.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-map api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="options"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#options" ariel-label="options" data-testid=":options">:options</a></code></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":options-desc"><span>Optional values that can be passed with a request.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-bool api-table-row" id="options-add_billing_address_to_payment_method"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#options-add_billing_address_to_payment_method" ariel-label="add_billing_address_to_payment_method" data-testid=":add_billing_address_to_payment_method">:add_billing_address_to_payment_method</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":add_billing_address_to_payment_method-type">bool</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":add_billing_address_to_payment_method-desc"><span>The option that determines whether the billing address information provided in the request should be added to the payment method specified. This will need to be set up even if the <code>account_type</code> parameter was passed in the corresponding 3D Secure call as it will not carry over.</p>
<p class=" markdown-p">Accepted account types are:</p>
<ul class=" list list--disc">
<li><code>credit</code> (default)</li>
<li><code>debit</code></li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="message message--note"><span class="message__title message__title--note">note</span><p class=" markdown-p">Some cards can be processed using either a credit or debit account and cardholders have the option to choose which account to process a transaction.</p></blockquote></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-bool api-table-row" id="options-hold_in_escrow"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#options-hold_in_escrow" ariel-label="hold_in_escrow" data-testid=":hold_in_escrow">:hold_in_escrow</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":hold_in_escrow-type">bool</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":hold_in_escrow-desc"><p>For Braintree Marketplace merchants only. <p class=" markdown-p"><em>We recommend using <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#transaction_source">transaction_source</a></code> with a value of <code>recurring</code>.</em></p>
<p class=" markdown-p">A value indicating whether the transaction is being passed with a recurring ecommerce indicator (ECI) flag. If passed, the amount submitted for settlement must exactly match the authorized amount.</p>
<p class=" markdown-p"><a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/articles/guides/fraud-tools/basic/avs-cvv-rules#how-avs-and-cvv-rules-work">AVS and CVV rules</a> do not apply to recurring payments.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-map api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="risk_data"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#risk_data" ariel-label="risk_data" data-testid=":risk_data">:risk_data</a></code></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":risk_data-desc"><p>Customer device information, which is sent directly to supported processors for fraud analysis. These fields are automatically populated if using <a href="/guides/premium-fraud-management-tools/overview">Premium Fraud Management Tools</a>. Currently only available when processing American Express via Amex Direct. <a href="/braintree/help?issue=TransactionProcessingQuestion">Contact us</a> with any questions.</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="risk_data-customer_browser"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#risk_data-customer_browser" ariel-label="customer_browser" data-testid=":customer_browser">:customer_browser</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":customer_browser-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":customer_browser-desc"><span>The <code>User-Agent</code> header provided by the customer&#x27;s browser, which gives information about the browser. Maximum 255 characters.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="risk_data-customer_ip"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#risk_data-customer_ip" ariel-label="customer_ip" data-testid=":customer_ip">:customer_ip</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":customer_ip-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":customer_ip-desc"><span>The customer&#x27;s IP address.</span></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="sca_exemption"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#sca_exemption" ariel-label="sca_exemption" data-testid=":sca_exemption">:sca_exemption</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":sca_exemption-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":sca_exemption-desc"><div><p>Specifies the Secure Customer Authentication exemption that this transaction will be claiming.</p><p>Accepted values:</p><ul><li><code>low_value</code></li><li><code>secure_corporate</code></li><li><code>trusted_beneficiary</code></li></ul></div></span></div></div><div class="type-decimal api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="service_fee_amount"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#service_fee_amount" ariel-label="service_fee_amount" data-testid=":service_fee_amount">:service_fee_amount</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":service_fee_amount-type">BigDecimal</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":service_fee_amount-desc"><div><p>The portion of a sub-merchant&#x27;s transaction revenue that is routed to the master merchant account. See <a href="/braintree/docs/guides/braintree-marketplace/create#holding-funds-in-escrow">charging a service fee and holding funds in escrow on Braintree Marketplace transactions</a>.</p></div></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="shared_billing_address_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#shared_billing_address_id" ariel-label="shared_billing_address_id" data-testid=":shared_billing_address_id">:shared_billing_address_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":shared_billing_address_id-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":shared_billing_address_id-desc"><p class=" markdown-p"><strong>For <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/guides/extend/oauth/shared-vault">Shared Vault</a> only</strong></p>
<p class=" markdown-p">The ID of an address belonging to the OAuth application owner. If used in conjunction with a <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#shared_customer_id">shared_customer_id</a></code>, must belong to the specified customer.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="shared_customer_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#shared_customer_id" ariel-label="shared_customer_id" data-testid=":shared_customer_id">:shared_customer_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":shared_customer_id-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":shared_customer_id-desc"><p class=" markdown-p"><strong>For <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/guides/extend/oauth/shared-vault">Shared Vault</a> only</strong></p>
<p class=" markdown-p">The ID of a customer belonging to the OAuth application owner.  If no <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#shared_payment_method_token">shared_payment_method_token</a></code> is specified, the customer&#x27;s default payment method will be used.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="shared_payment_method_nonce"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#shared_payment_method_nonce" ariel-label="shared_payment_method_nonce" data-testid=":shared_payment_method_nonce">:shared_payment_method_nonce</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":shared_payment_method_nonce-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":shared_payment_method_nonce-desc"><p class=" markdown-p"><strong>For <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/guides/extend/oauth/shared-vault">Shared Vault</a> only</strong></p>
<p class=" markdown-p">A payment method nonce belonging to the OAuth application owner. These payment method nonces can be credit cards or channel-initiated PayPal Billing Agreements that have been executed. Mutually exclusive with <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#shared_payment_method_token">shared_payment_method_token</a></code>.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="shared_payment_method_token"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#shared_payment_method_token" ariel-label="shared_payment_method_token" data-testid=":shared_payment_method_token">:shared_payment_method_token</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":shared_payment_method_token-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":shared_payment_method_token-desc"><p class=" markdown-p"><strong>For <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/guides/extend/oauth/shared-vault">Shared Vault</a> only</strong></p>
<p class=" markdown-p">The token of a payment method belonging to the OAuth application owner. Mutually exclusive with <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#shared_payment_method_nonce">shared_payment_method_nonce</a></code>. If no <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#shared_customer_id">shared_customer_id</a></code> is explicitly specified, the customer that owns the payment method is implicitly specified. If used in conjunction with a <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#shared_customer_id">shared_customer_id</a></code>, must belong to the specified customer.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="shared_shipping_address_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#shared_shipping_address_id" ariel-label="shared_shipping_address_id" data-testid=":shared_shipping_address_id">:shared_shipping_address_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":shared_shipping_address_id-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":shared_shipping_address_id-desc"><p class=" markdown-p"><strong>For <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/guides/extend/oauth/shared-vault">Shared Vault</a> only</strong></p>
<p class=" markdown-p">The ID of an address belonging to the OAuth application owner. If used in conjunction with a <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#shared_customer_id">shared_customer_id</a></code>, must belong to the specified customer.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-map api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="shipping"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#shipping" ariel-label="shipping" data-testid=":shipping">:shipping</a></code></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":shipping-desc"><span>Shipping address information associated with a specific customer ID.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="shipping-company"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#shipping-company" ariel-label="company" data-testid=":company">:company</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":company-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":company-desc"><span>Company name. 255 character maximum.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="shipping-country_code_alpha2"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#shipping-country_code_alpha2" ariel-label="country_code_alpha2" data-testid=":country_code_alpha2">:country_code_alpha2</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":country_code_alpha2-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":country_code_alpha2-desc"><p>The <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_3166-1_alpha-2">ISO 3166-1 alpha-2</a> country code specified in an address. Canada: ANA[space]NAN</li></ul></div></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="shipping-region"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#shipping-region" ariel-label="region" data-testid=":region">:region</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":region-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":region-desc"><span>The state or province. </li>

The maximum number of addresses per customer is 50.</span></span></div></div><div class="type-decimal api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="shipping_amount"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#shipping_amount" ariel-label="shipping_amount" data-testid=":shipping_amount">:shipping_amount</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":shipping_amount-type">BigDecimal</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":shipping_amount-desc"><p>A <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/level-2-and-3-processing/required-fields#level-3-data">Level 3 field</a> that specifies the shipping cost on the entire transaction. US: Can be provided in this format:</p><ul><li>5 digits (ex: 10001)</li><li>5 digits + 4 digits (ex: 100010000)</li><li>5 digits + &quot;-&quot; + 4 digits (ex: 10001-0000)
Canada: ANA[space]NAN</li></ul></div></span></div></div><div class="type-decimal api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="surcharge_amount"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#surcharge_amount" ariel-label="surcharge_amount" data-testid=":surcharge_amount">:surcharge_amount</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":surcharge_amount-type">BigDecimal</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":surcharge_amount-desc"><span>The data field that specifies the surcharge amount that was included in the total transaction amount.
