Your merchant account must be registered for surcharging.</span></span></div></div><div class="type-decimal api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="tax_amount"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#tax_amount" ariel-label="tax_amount" data-testid=":tax_amount">:tax_amount</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":tax_amount-type">BigDecimal</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":tax_amount-desc"><p>A <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/level-2-and-3-processing/required-fields#level-2-data">Level 2 field</a> that specifies the amount of tax that was included in the total transaction amount. The value can&#x27;t be negative, and in most cases, it must be greater than zero in order to qualify for lower interchange rates. It does not add to the total transaction amount. For the US Visa CEDP, the tax amount should be calculated according to the total transaction amount, if tax was collected. Tax estimation is not allowed.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-bool api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="tax_exempt"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#tax_exempt" ariel-label="tax_exempt" data-testid=":tax_exempt">:tax_exempt</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":tax_exempt-type">bool</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":tax_exempt-desc"><p>A <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/level-2-and-3-processing/required-fields#level-2-data">Level 2 field</a> that indicates whether or not the transaction should be considered eligible for tax exemption. This does not affect the total transaction amount.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="three_d_secure_authentication_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#three_d_secure_authentication_id" ariel-label="three_d_secure_authentication_id" data-testid=":three_d_secure_authentication_id">:three_d_secure_authentication_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":three_d_secure_authentication_id-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":three_d_secure_authentication_id-desc"><span>ID of the 3D Secure authentication performed for this transaction. Do not provide this field if you are using a nonce for this transaction that is 3D Secure enriched.</span></span></div></div><div class="type-map api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="three_d_secure_pass_thru"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#three_d_secure_pass_thru" ariel-label="three_d_secure_pass_thru" data-testid=":three_d_secure_pass_thru">:three_d_secure_pass_thru</a></code></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":three_d_secure_pass_thru-desc"><p>Results of a merchant-performed 3D Secure authentication. <strong>You will only need to use these fields if you&#x27;ve performed your own integration with a 3D Secure MPI provider (e.g. Cardinal Centinel).</strong> Otherwise, Braintree&#x27;s SDKs handle this for you in <a href="/braintree/docs/guides/3d-secure/overview">our standard 3D Secure integration</a>.</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="three_d_secure_pass_thru-cavv"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#three_d_secure_pass_thru-cavv" ariel-label="cavv" data-testid=":cavv">:cavv</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":cavv-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":cavv-desc"><p class=" markdown-p">Cardholder authentication verification value or CAVV. The main
encrypted message issuers and card networks use to verify authentication
has occurred. Mastercard uses an AVV message and American Express uses an
AEVV message, each of which should also be passed in the <span class="langAttribute">cavv</span>
parameter.</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="three_d_secure_pass_thru-directory_response"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#three_d_secure_pass_thru-directory_response" ariel-label="directory_response" data-testid=":directory_response">:directory_response</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":directory_response-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":directory_response-desc"><span>The TransStatus from the 3D Secure provider. This will be a single character such as Y, N, or other values.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="three_d_secure_pass_thru-ds_transaction_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#three_d_secure_pass_thru-ds_transaction_id" ariel-label="ds_transaction_id" data-testid=":ds_transaction_id">:ds_transaction_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":ds_transaction_id-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":ds_transaction_id-desc"><p>Transaction identifier resulting from 3D Secure 2 authentication. This
field must be supplied for Mastercard Identity Check.</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="three_d_secure_pass_thru-eci_flag"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#three_d_secure_pass_thru-eci_flag" ariel-label="eci_flag" data-testid=":eci_flag">:eci_flag</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":eci_flag-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":eci_flag-desc"><div><p>The value of the electronic commerce indicator (ECI) flag, which indicates the outcome of the 3DS authentication.</p><p>Accepted values for Mastercard:</p><ul><li><code>00</code> = Failed or not attempted</li><li><code>01</code> = Attempted</li><li><code>02</code> = Success</li><li><code>04</code> = Data-Only (Applies to limited processors)</li></ul><p>Accepted values for all other card brands:</p><ul><li><code>07</code> = Failed or not attempted</li><li><code>06</code> = Attempted</li><li><code>05</code> = Success</li></ul></div></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="three_d_secure_pass_thru-three_d_secure_version"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#three_d_secure_pass_thru-three_d_secure_version" ariel-label="three_d_secure_version" data-testid=":three_d_secure_version">:three_d_secure_version</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":three_d_secure_version-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":three_d_secure_version-desc"><p>The version of 3D Secure authentication used for the transaction. Required
on Visa and Mastercard authentications. Must be composed of digits separated
by periods (e.g. <code>1.0.2</code>).</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="three_d_secure_pass_thru-xid"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#three_d_secure_pass_thru-xid" ariel-label="xid" data-testid=":xid">:xid</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":xid-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":xid-desc"><p>Transaction identifier resulting from 3D Secure authentication. Uniquely
identifies the transaction and sometimes required in the authorization
message. Must be base64-encoded. This field will no longer be used in
3D Secure 2 authentications.</p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="transaction_source"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#transaction_source" ariel-label="transaction_source" data-testid=":transaction_source">:transaction_source</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":transaction_source-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":transaction_source-desc"><div><p>Specifies the source of the transaction. The value passed depends on whether the transaction is initiated by the merchant or the customer. If the transaction is an ecommerce transaction initiated by the customer, no value is passed.</p><p>Accepted values for merchant-initiated transactions:</p><ul><li><code>recurring</code> = Transactions for subsequent recurring payments (e.g. subscriptions with a fixed amount on a predefined schedule).</li><li><code>unscheduled</code> = Transactions for unscheduled payments that are not recurring on a predefined schedule or amount (e.g. balance top-up). Formerly <code>merchant</code>.</li><li><code>installment</code> = Transactions for subsequent installment payments. (e.g. when the customer makes a single large purchase and wants to make payments over time).</li></ul><p>Accepted values for customer-initiated transactions:</p><ul><li><code>recurring_first</code> = Transactions that represent the first in a series of recurring payments or subscription.</li><li><code>moto</code> = Transactions that are initiated by the customer via the merchant by mail or telephone.</li><li><code>installment_first</code> = Transactions that represent the first in a series of installment payments.</li><li><code>estimated</code> = Transactions that support subsequent incremental authorization.</li><li>&#x27;estimated_moto&#x27; =  Transactions that are initiated by the customer via the merchant by mail or telephone that support subsequent incremental authorization.</li></ul><p>Note: <code>installment</code> and <code>installment_first</code> may only be available in certain regions.  If installment transactions are not supported in your region, the transaction will automatically be categorized as <code>recurring</code>.</p><p><a href="https://www.braintreepayments.com/blog/visa-stored-credential-framework-processing-improvements-for-vaulted-cards/">Learn more about the Visa Stored Credential Framework in our blog.</a></p></div></span></div></div><div class="type-map api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="us_bank_account"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#us_bank_account" ariel-label="us_bank_account" data-testid=":us_bank_account">:us_bank_account</a></code></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":us_bank_account-desc"><span>Details associated with a customer&#x27;s US bank account to be used for the transaction.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="us_bank_account-ach_mandate_accepted_at"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#us_bank_account-ach_mandate_accepted_at" ariel-label="ach_mandate_accepted_at" data-testid=":ach_mandate_accepted_at">:ach_mandate_accepted_at</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":ach_mandate_accepted_at-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":ach_mandate_accepted_at-desc"><span>The date and time the ACH mandate was accepted in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601">ISO 8601</a> format.</span></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row" id="us_bank_account-ach_mandate_text"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#us_bank_account-ach_mandate_text" ariel-label="ach_mandate_text" data-testid=":ach_mandate_text">:ach_mandate_text</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name" data-testid=":ach_mandate_text-type">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description" data-testid=":ach_mandate_text-desc"><span>The text of the ACH mandate.</span></span></div></div></div>;<h2 id="examples" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Examples</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#examples" aria-label="Examples"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><h3 id="full-example" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Full example</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#full-example" aria-label="Full example"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><span>
    Here is an example of passing in everything a typical merchant might use. </span><p class="markdown-p"></p><span>Some parameters are
    mutually exclusive, so we'll show those in separate examples. If there is anything you want to store
    with the transaction details that we don't have a field for, you can always use
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#custom_fields"><span>custom fields</span></a><span>.</span><p class="markdown-p"></p><a href="/braintree/docs/guides/premium-fraud-management-tools/client-side"><span>Collect device data</span></a><span>
    from the client and include the </span><span class="langAttribute">device_data_from_the_client</span><span> in the
    transaction.

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :amount =&gt; &quot;100.00&quot;,
    :order_id =&gt; &quot;order id&quot;,
    :merchant_account_id =&gt; &quot;a_merchant_account_id&quot;,
    :payment_method_nonce =&gt; nonce_from_the_client,
    :device_data =&gt; device_data_from_the_client,
    :customer =&gt; {
        :first_name =&gt; &quot;Drew&quot;,
        :last_name =&gt; &quot;Smith&quot;,
        :company =&gt; &quot;Braintree&quot;,
        :phone =&gt; &quot;312-555-1234&quot;,
        :fax =&gt; &quot;312-555-1235&quot;,
        :website =&gt; &quot;http://www.example.com&quot;,
        :email =&gt; &quot;<a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="8ce8fee9fbcce9f4ede1fce0e9a2efe3e1">[email&#160;protected]</a>&quot;
    },
    :billing =&gt; {
        :first_name =&gt; &quot;Paul&quot;,
        :last_name =&gt; &quot;Smith&quot;,
        :company =&gt; &quot;Braintree&quot;,
        :street_address =&gt; &quot;1 E Main St&quot;,
        :extended_address =&gt; &quot;Suite 403&quot;,
        :locality =&gt; &quot;Chicago&quot;,
        :region =&gt; &quot;IL&quot;,
        :postal_code =&gt; &quot;60622&quot;,
        :country_code_alpha2 =&gt; &quot;US&quot;
    },
    :shipping =&gt; {
        :first_name =&gt; &quot;Jen&quot;,
        :last_name =&gt; &quot;Smith&quot;,
        :company =&gt; &quot;Braintree&quot;,
        :street_address =&gt; &quot;1 E 1st St&quot;,
        :extended_address =&gt; &quot;Suite 403&quot;,
        :locality =&gt; &quot;Bartlett&quot;,
        :region =&gt; &quot;IL&quot;,
        :postal_code =&gt; &quot;60103&quot;,
        :country_code_alpha2 =&gt; &quot;US&quot;
    },
    :options =&gt; {
        :submit_for_settlement =&gt; true
    }
)</code></pre></div></div><span>

    If all the parameters are valid, a transaction will be created with a status of
    submitted_for_settlement and success? will return true.

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result.success? //=&gt; true
result.transaction.type //=&gt; &quot;credit&quot;
result.transaction.status //=&gt; &quot;submitted_for_settlement&quot;</code></pre></div></div><h3 id="storing-in-vault" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Storing in Vault</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#storing-in-vault" aria-label="Storing in Vault"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><span>
    When creating a transaction, you can also store the payment method in your Vault.
    </span><h4 id="existing-customer-with-new-payment-method" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>Existing customer with new payment method</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#existing-customer-with-new-payment-method" aria-label="Existing customer with new payment method"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><span>
    To associate this transaction's payment method with an existing customer, pass a
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#customer_id"><span class="langAttribute">customer_id</span></a><span> along with
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#options-store_in_vault"><span class="langAttribute">options.store_in_vault</span></a><span> or
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#options-store_in_vault_on_success"><span class="langAttribute">options.store_in_vault_on_success</span></a><span>
    as </span><span class="langAttribute">true</span><span>.

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :amount =&gt; &quot;10.00&quot;,
    :payment_method_nonce =&gt; nonce_from_the_client,
    :customer_id =&gt; &quot;the_customer_id&quot;,
    :options =&gt; {
        :store_in_vault_on_success =&gt; true
    }
)</code></pre></div></div><h4 id="new-customer-with-new-payment-method" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>New customer with new payment method</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#new-customer-with-new-payment-method" aria-label="New customer with new payment method"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><span>
    To store a payment method for a new customer, set
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#options-store_in_vault"><span class="langAttribute">options.store_in_vault</span></a><span> or
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#options-store_in_vault_on_success"><span class="langAttribute">options.store_in_vault_on_success</span></a><span>
    to </span><span class="langAttribute">true</span><span> on your transaction. You can optionally specify
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#customer"><span class="langAttribute">customer</span></a><span> parameters for your new customer, as
    well:

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :amount =&gt; &quot;10.00&quot;,
    :payment_method_nonce =&gt; nonce_from_the_client,
    :customer =&gt; {
        :id =&gt; &quot;a_customer_id&quot;
    },
    :options =&gt; {
        :store_in_vault_on_success =&gt; true
    }
)</code></pre></div></div><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><style data-emotion="css 4757ty-svg-size_xs">.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs{speak:none;display:inline-block;aspect-ratio:1;width:1.125rem;height:1.125rem;}.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs img,.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs svg{width:100%;height:100%;display:block;}</style><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__title__FOcbD">Note</span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
        The </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#customer"><span class="langAttribute">customer</span></a><span> parameter should only be used when
        creating a new customer with a new payment method, and
        </span><span class="langAttribute">store_in_vault_on_success</span><span> only vaults the payment method if the
        transaction is successful.
    </span></span></div></div><h3 id="using-a-vaulted-payment-method" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Using a vaulted payment method</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#using-a-vaulted-payment-method" aria-label="Using a vaulted payment method"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><span>
    You can create a transaction using a payment method stored in the
    </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/vault/overview"><span>Vault</span></a><span> by passing a
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#payment_method_token"><span class="langAttribute">payment_method_token</span></a><span>:

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :payment_method_token =&gt; &quot;the_token&quot;,
    :amount =&gt; &quot;10.00&quot;
)</code></pre></div></div><span>

    Or use </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#customer_id"><span class="langAttribute">customer_id</span></a><span>, which will use the
    customer's default payment method:

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :customer_id =&gt; &quot;the_customer_id&quot;,
    :amount =&gt; &quot;10.00&quot;
)</code></pre></div></div><h3 id="using-a-cvv-only-nonce" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Using a CVV-only nonce</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#using-a-cvv-only-nonce" aria-label="Using a CVV-only nonce"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><span>
    To transact with a CVV-only nonce, use both a nonce representing the CVV </span><strong><span>and</span></strong><span> a
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#payment_method_token"><span class="langAttribute">payment_method_token</span></a><span> representing the
    vaulted payment method.</span><p class="markdown-p"></p><span> To collect a CVV-only nonce, use the client SDKs to tokenize only the CVV
    property. See an example in our
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/guides/hosted-fields/faq/javascript/v3#can-i-verify-the-cvv-when-a-customer-uses-or-updates-a-vaulted-card?"><span>Hosted Fields FAQ</span></a><span>.

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :payment_method_token =&gt; &quot;the_token&quot;,
    :payment_method_nonce =&gt; cvvOnlyNonceFromClient,
    :amount =&gt; &quot;10.00&quot;
)</code></pre></div></div><h3 id="specify-merchant-account-id" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Specify merchant account ID</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#specify-merchant-account-id" aria-label="Specify merchant account ID"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><span>
    To specify which merchant account to use, pass the
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#merchant_account_id"><span class="langAttribute">merchant_account_id</span></a><span> when creating the
    transaction.

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :amount =&gt; &quot;10.00&quot;,
    :merchant_account_id =&gt; &quot;your_merchant_account&quot;,
    :payment_method_nonce =&gt; nonce_from_the_client
)</code></pre></div></div><span>

    If you don't specify the merchant account to use to process a transaction, Braintree will process it
    using your default merchant account.</span><p class="markdown-p"></p><a href="/braintree/help?issue=TransactionProcessingQuestion"><span>Contact us</span></a><span> if you would like to
    change which merchant account is default.
    </span><h3 id="using-stored-addresses" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Using stored addresses</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#using-stored-addresses" aria-label="Using stored addresses"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><span>
    You can use
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/address/create"><span>addresses stored on a customer</span></a><span> by
    passing the address's ID. This works for both the shipping address and billing address.

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :customer_id =&gt; &quot;the_customer_id&quot;,
    :amount =&gt; &quot;10.00&quot;,
    :billing_address_id =&gt; &quot;AA&quot;,
    :shipping_address_id =&gt; &quot;AB&quot;
)</code></pre></div></div><h3 id="custom-fields" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Custom fields</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#custom-fields" aria-label="Custom fields"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><span>
    Whatever you
    </span><a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/custom-fields#creating-a-custom-field"><span>configure as the API name for your custom fields</span></a><span>
    will be used when setting them on the transaction. Here is an example of setting custom fields with
    API names of </span><code><span>custom_field_one</span></code><span> and </span><code><span>custom_field_two</span></code><span>.

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :amount =&gt; &quot;10.00&quot;,
    :payment_method_nonce =&gt; nonce_from_the_client,
    :custom_fields =&gt; {
        :custom_field_one =&gt; &quot;value one&quot;,
        :custom_field_two =&gt; &quot;value two&quot;
    }
)
if result.success? {
    result.transaction.custom_fields //=&gt; {:custom_field_one =&gt; &quot;value one&quot;, :custom_field_two =&gt; &quot;value two&quot;}
}</code></pre></div></div><h3 id="dynamic-descriptors" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Dynamic descriptors</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#dynamic-descriptors" aria-label="Dynamic descriptors"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><span>
    Dynamic descriptors are typically composed of a name and phone number or URL. The name must include
    the business name, followed by a product name or identifier, separated by an asterisk (*). Depending
    on the type of transaction you're creating, the length/character limits may differ from those
    outlined above. For example, you can only specify up to 18 characters for dynamic descriptor names
    on Braintree Marketplace transactions. See below for details on </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#venmo"><span>Venmo</span></a><span>,
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#paypal"><span>PayPal</span></a><span>, and </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#braintree-marketplace"><span>Braintree Marketplace</span></a><span> dynamic
    descriptors.</span><p class="markdown-p"></p><span> Your processor may also restrict which descriptor values you can pass; certain
    processors allow you to pass URLs instead of phone numbers, while others accept only phone numbers
    or only names. If your processor supports URLs and you send both a phone number and URL, we will
    only pass the URL to the processor.
    </span><a href="/braintree/help?issue=updateDescriptor"><span>Contact us</span></a><span> for more information on your
    processor's specific requirements.

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :amount =&gt; &quot;10.00&quot;,
    :payment_method_nonce =&gt; nonce_from_the_client,
    :descriptor =&gt; {
        :name =&gt; &quot;company*my product&quot;,
        :phone =&gt; &quot;3125551212&quot;,
        :url =&gt; &quot;company.com&quot;
    }
)
&lt;a href=&quot;http://result.transaction.descriptor.name&quot;&gt;result.transaction.descriptor.name&lt;/a&gt; //=&gt; &quot;company*my product&quot;
result.transaction.descriptor.phone //=&gt; &quot;3125551212&quot;</code></pre></div></div><h4 id="venmo" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>Venmo</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#venmo" aria-label="Venmo"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><span>
    Venmo only supports the dynamic descriptor </span><code><span>name</span></code><span>. Its format allows alpha-numeric
    characters and </span><code><span>+-. </span></code><span> (space included); any other characters will result in the dynamic
    descriptor name not being included in the full descriptor sent to the processor.</span><p class="markdown-p"></p><span> The full descriptor
    submitted to the processor is structured as follows:</span><p class="markdown-p"></p><ul class="list list--disc"><li><span>
            The default prefix of
            </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list styles_tab_list_no_label"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active"></li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-bash"><code class="language-bash">VENMO  *</code></pre></div></div><span>
            (Two whitespaces).
        </span></li><li><span>
            The </span><code><span>Business Name</span></code><span> submitted in the
            </span><a href="/braintree/articles/guides/payment-methods/venmo#go-live"><span>Venmo application form</span></a><span>.
        </span></li><li><span>
            The </span><code><span>Dynamic Descriptor Name</span></code><span> submitted in the
            </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/#descriptor-name"><span>transaction.sale()</span></a><span> or

            </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/submit-for-settlement/ruby#descriptor"><span>transaction.submit_for_settlement()</span></a><span>
            call.
        </span></li></ul><span>
    An example of a full descriptor with a valid dynamic descriptor name is: VENMO *AStore O-1234, where
    </span><code><span>AStore</span></code><span> is the </span><code><span>Business Name</span></code><span> and </span><code><span>O-1234</span></code><span> is the
    </span><code><span>Dynamic Descriptor Name</span></code><span>. If the dynamic descriptor name contains invalid characters,
    e.g. 0#1234, the entire dynamic descriptor name will be ignored.

    </span><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><style data-emotion="css 4757ty-svg-size_xs">.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs{speak:none;display:inline-block;aspect-ratio:1;width:1.125rem;height:1.125rem;}.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs img,.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs svg{width:100%;height:100%;display:block;}</style><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__title__FOcbD">Note</span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
        The full descriptor is limited to 22 characters. If this limit is exceeded, the
        </span><code><span>Business Name</span></code><span> and </span><code><span>Dynamic Descriptor Name</span></code><span> portion will be truncated as
        needed. If you want to change the </span><code><span>Business Name</span></code><span> of the descriptor, you can edit your
        Venmo profile via the Venmo Processing page in the Control Panel. This will also update the name
        displayed to customers in the Venmo app during transaction processing.
    </span></span></div></div><h4 id="paypal" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>PayPal</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#paypal" aria-label="PayPal"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><span>
    For PayPal transactions only, the dynamic descriptor is limited to a total of 22 characters and includes the following
    elements:</span><p class="markdown-p"></p><ul class="list list--disc"><li><span>The default prefix of </span><code><span>PAYPAL *</span></code></li><li><span>Your PayPal hard descriptor*</span></li><li><span>The product portion of your </span><code><span>name</span></code></li></ul><p class="markdown-p"><span>These rules apply only when the payment method is PayPal. Card and other payment methods follow their own descriptor rules.</span></p><em><span>*Depending on your PayPal account setup, the PayPal hard descriptor may not be included in the
        dynamic descriptor. You can update the hard descriptor value from your
    </span></em><a href="https://www.paypal.com/login"><span>PayPal console</span></a><span>.</span><p class="markdown-p"></p><span>
    They&nbsp;</span><span class="langAttribute">name</span><span> must meet the following guidelines:</span><p class="markdown-p"></p><ul class="list list--disc"><li><span>
            Must include your registered Doing Business As (DBA) name, followed by an asterisk and a product
            description
        </span></li><li><span>
            The DBA portion must be 3, 7 or 12 characters long - this portion will be dropped from your
            dynamic descriptor
        </span></li></ul><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><style data-emotion="css 4757ty-svg-size_xs">.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs{speak:none;display:inline-block;aspect-ratio:1;width:1.125rem;height:1.125rem;}.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs img,.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs svg{width:100%;height:100%;display:block;}</style><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__title__FOcbD">Note</span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
        If the three parts of your dynamic descriptor combined exceed the 22 character limit, the
        </span><span class="langAttribute">name</span><span> portion will automatically be truncated as needed.
    </span></span></div></div><span>

    The payment information displayed to a customer in their PayPal account overview does not contain
    the dynamic descriptor. The information displayed there is data the merchant has configured with
    PayPal directly (e.g. business name, email address, business contact details).
    </span><h4 id="braintree-marketplace" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>Braintree Marketplace</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#braintree-marketplace" aria-label="Braintree Marketplace"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><span>
    The only dynamic descriptor value we will pass for Braintree Marketplace transactions is the
    </span><span class="langAttribute">name</span><span> you specify. We will not send any dynamic
    </span><span class="langAttribute">phone</span><span> or </span><span class="langAttribute">url</span><span> values to the processor, but we
    will pass the </span><span class="langAttribute">phone</span><span> from the hard descriptor on your master merchant
    account. </span><p class="markdown-p"></p><span>The dynamic descriptor name can only contain the ASCII characters a-z, A-Z, the numbers
    0-9, and the characters </span><code><span>.-+</span></code><span> and spaces (it can't contain special characters like
    </span><code><span></span></code><span>, </span><code><span></span></code><span>, and </span><code><span></span></code><span>). The maximum length is 18 characters; we will
    truncate any longer strings. The descriptor we pass to the processor will start with
    </span><code><span>"BT *"</span></code><span>, followed by the </span><span class="langAttribute">name</span><span> you specify.</span><p class="markdown-p"></p><ul class="list list--disc"><li><span>
            If the specified name is 12 characters or fewer, the descriptor we pass to the processor will
            end with a randomly generated 6-character string (e.g. </span><code><span>123abc</span></code><span>) which identifies the
            sub-merchant:
            </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list styles_tab_list_no_label"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active"></li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-html"><code class="language-html">BT *MYDESCRIPTOR123abc</code></pre></div></div></li><li><span>
            If the specified name is 13 characters or greater, the descriptor we pass to the processor will
            not end with a randomly generated 6-character string:
            </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list styles_tab_list_no_label"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active"></li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-html"><code class="language-html">BT *MYDESCRIPTORISLONG</code></pre></div></div></li></ul><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><style data-emotion="css 4757ty-svg-size_xs">.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs{speak:none;display:inline-block;aspect-ratio:1;width:1.125rem;height:1.125rem;}.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs img,.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs svg{width:100%;height:100%;display:block;}</style><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__title__FOcbD">Note</span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
        The sub-merchant can't access the 6-character stringwe automatically append it to the descriptor
        name after you submit the transaction request. The string can't be changed, as it is required in
        order to identify each transaction we process for the sub-merchant.
    </span></span></div></div><h3 id="hold-a-braintree-marketplace-transaction-in-escrow-on-creation" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Hold a Braintree Marketplace transaction in escrow on creation</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#hold-a-braintree-marketplace-transaction-in-escrow-on-creation" aria-label="Hold a Braintree Marketplace transaction in escrow on creation"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><span>
    Upon creating a
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/guides/braintree-marketplace/create"><span>Braintree Marketplace transaction</span></a><span>,
    you can specify that its funds should be held in escrow. These funds can then be
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/release-from-escrow"><span>released</span></a><span> at your
    discretion. By default, funds are not held in escrow.

    </span><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result = gateway.transaction.sale(
    :amount =&gt; &quot;100.00&quot;,
    :merchant_account_id =&gt; &quot;blue_ladders_store&quot;,
    :payment_method_nonce =&gt; nonce_from_the_client,
    :options =&gt; {
        :submit_for_settlement =&gt; true,
        :hold_in_escrow =&gt; true
    },
    :service_fee_amount =&gt; &quot;10.00&quot;
)</code></pre></div></div></section></div><nav class="right-nav-container"><h4 class="right-nav-title">On this page</h4><ul class="right-nav-list"></ul></nav></div></article></main><div><footer       :hold_in_escrow =\u003e true\n    },\n    :service_fee_amount =\u003e Sale\nslug: /docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby/\ncreateTime: '2025-04-02T01:08:48.880Z'\nupdateTime: '2025-12-12T20:26:53.926Z'\n---\n\n\n# Transaction: Sale\n\nSee also the[Transaction](/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction)response object.\n\nTo create a transaction, you must include an[`amount`](#amount)and either a[`payment_method_nonce`](#payment_method_nonce), a[`payment_method_token`](#payment_method_token), or a[`customer_id`](#customer_id). Passing a`customer_id`is equivalent to passing the`payment_method_token`of the customer's default payment method.\n\nBraintree offers products that manage risk and fraud related to each transaction. These products can only be leveraged if there is adequate data to support the capabilities. The required data can be easily added during the Braintree SDK or[Graph QL](/braintree/graphql/). integration, and must be done prior using risk products. For additional guidance go to[Premium Fraud Management Tools](/braintree/articles/guides/fraud-tools/premium/overview).\n\nThe following example creates a transaction using a[`payment_method_nonce`](#payment_method_nonce)from a client and instructs that it should be submitted for settlement immediately using[`options.submit_for_settlement`](#options-submit_for_settlement). You can see more[examples](#examples), including[using a vaulted payment method](#using-a-vaulted-payment-method), below the parameter reference.\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :amount =\u003e \"10.00\",\n    :payment_method_nonce =\u003e nonce_from_the_client,\n    :device_data =\u003e device_data_from_the_client,\n    :options =\u003e {\n        :submit_for_settlement =\u003e true\n    }\n)\nif result.success? {\n    // See result.transaction for details\n} else {\n    // Handle errors\n}\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n\n### Full example\n\nHere is an example of passing in everything a typical merchant might use.\n\nSome parameters are mutually exclusive, so we'll show those in separate examples. If there is anything you want to store with the transaction details that we don't have a field for, you can always use[custom fields](#custom_fields).\n\n[Collect device data](/braintree/docs/guides/premium-fraud-management-tools/client-side)from the client and include the`device_data_from_the_client`in the transaction.\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :amount =\u003e \"100.00\",\n    :order_id =\u003e \"order id\",\n    :merchant_account_id =\u003e \"a_merchant_account_id\",\n    :payment_method_nonce =\u003e nonce_from_the_client,\n    :device_data =\u003e device_data_from_the_client,\n    :customer =\u003e {\n        :first_name =\u003e \"Drew\",\n        :last_name =\u003e \"Smith\",\n        :company =\u003e \"Braintree\",\n        :phone =\u003e \"312-555-1234\",\n        :fax =\u003e \"312-555-1235\",\n        :website =\u003e \"http://www.example.com\",\n        :email =\u003e \"drew@example.com\"\n    },\n    :billing =\u003e {\n        :first_name =\u003e \"Paul\",\n        :last_name =\u003e \"Smith\",\n        :company =\u003e \"Braintree\",\n        :street_address =\u003e \"1 E Main St\",\n        :extended_address =\u003e \"Suite 403\",\n        :locality =\u003e \"Chicago\",\n        :region =\u003e \"IL\",\n        :postal_code =\u003e \"60622\",\n        :country_code_alpha2 =\u003e \"US\"\n    },\n    :shipping =\u003e {\n        :first_name =\u003e \"Jen\",\n        :last_name =\u003e \"Smith\",\n        :company =\u003e \"Braintree\",\n        :street_address =\u003e \"1 E 1st St\",\n        :extended_address =\u003e \"Suite 403\",\n        :locality =\u003e \"Bartlett\",\n        :region =\u003e \"IL\",\n        :postal_code =\u003e \"60103\",\n        :country_code_alpha2 =\u003e \"US\"\n    },\n    :options =\u003e {\n        :submit_for_settlement =\u003e true\n    }\n)\n```\nIf all the parameters are valid, a transaction will be created with a status of submitted_for_settlement and success? will return true.\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult.success? //=\u003e true\nresult.transaction.type //=\u003e \"credit\"\nresult.transaction.status //=\u003e \"submitted_for_settlement\"\n```\n\n### Storing in Vault\n\nWhen creating a transaction, you can also store the payment method in your Vault.\n#### Existing customer with new payment method\n\nTo associate this transaction's payment method with an existing customer, pass a[`customer_id`](#customer_id)along with[`options.store_in_vault`](#options-store_in_vault)or[`options.store_in_vault_on_success`](#options-store_in_vault_on_success)as`true`.\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :amount =\u003e \"10.00\",\n    :payment_method_nonce =\u003e nonce_from_the_client,\n    :customer_id =\u003e \"the_customer_id\",\n    :options =\u003e {\n        :store_in_vault_on_success =\u003e true\n    }\n)\n```\n\n#### New customer with new payment method\n\nTo store a payment method for a new customer, set[`options.store_in_vault`](#options-store_in_vault)or[`options.store_in_vault_on_success`](#options-store_in_vault_on_success)to`true`on your transaction. You can optionally specify[`customer`](#customer)parameters for your new customer, as well:\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :amount =\u003e \"10.00\",\n    :payment_method_nonce =\u003e nonce_from_the_client,\n    :customer =\u003e {\n        :id =\u003e \"a_customer_id\"\n    },\n    :options =\u003e {\n        :store_in_vault_on_success =\u003e true\n    }\n)\n```\n\n**NOTE**\nThe [`customer`](#customer) parameter should only be used when creating a new customer with a new payment method, and `store_in_vault_on_success` only vaults the payment method if the transaction is successful.\n\n\n### Using a vaulted payment method\n\nYou can create a transaction using a payment method stored in the[Vault](/braintree/articles/control-panel/vault/overview)by passing a[`payment_method_token`](#payment_method_token):\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :payment_method_token =\u003e \"the_token\",\n    :amount =\u003e \"10.00\"\n)\n```\nOr use[`customer_id`](#customer_id), which will use the customer's default payment method:\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :customer_id =\u003e \"the_customer_id\",\n    :amount =\u003e \"10.00\"\n)\n```\n\n### Using a CVV-only nonce\n\nTo transact with a CVV-only nonce, use both a nonce representing the CVV**and**a[`payment_method_token`](#payment_method_token)representing the vaulted payment method.\n\nTo collect a CVV-only nonce, use the client SDKs to tokenize only the CVV property. See an example in our[Hosted Fields FAQ](/braintree/docs/guides/hosted-fields/faq/javascript/v3#can-i-verify-the-cvv-when-a-customer-uses-or-updates-a-vaulted-card?).\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :payment_method_token =\u003e \"the_token\",\n    :payment_method_nonce =\u003e cvvOnlyNonceFromClient,\n    :amount =\u003e \"10.00\"\n)\n```\n\n### Specify merchant account ID\n\nTo specify which merchant account to use, pass the[`merchant_account_id`](#merchant_account_id)when creating the transaction.\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :amount =\u003e \"10.00\",\n    :merchant_account_id =\u003e \"your_merchant_account\",\n    :payment_method_nonce =\u003e nonce_from_the_client\n)\n```\nIf you don't specify the merchant account to use to process a transaction, Braintree will process it using your default merchant account.\n\n[Contact us](/braintree/help?issue=TransactionProcessingQuestion)if you would like to change which merchant account is default.\n### Using stored addresses\n\nYou can use[addresses stored on a customer](/braintree/docs/reference/request/address/create)by passing the address's ID. This works for both the shipping address and billing address.\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :customer_id =\u003e \"the_customer_id\",\n    :amount =\u003e \"10.00\",\n    :billing_address_id =\u003e \"AA\",\n    :shipping_address_id =\u003e \"AB\"\n)\n```\n\n### Custom fields\n\nWhatever you[configure as the API name for your custom fields](/braintree/articles/control-panel/custom-fields#creating-a-custom-field)will be used when setting them on the transaction. Here is an example of setting custom fields with API names ofcustom_field_oneandcustom_field_two.\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :amount =\u003e \"10.00\",\n    :payment_method_nonce =\u003e nonce_from_the_client,\n    :custom_fields =\u003e {\n        :custom_field_one =\u003e \"value one\",\n        :custom_field_two =\u003e \"value two\"\n    }\n)\nif result.success? {\n    result.transaction.custom_fields //=\u003e {:custom_field_one =\u003e \"value one\", :custom_field_two =\u003e \"value two\"}\n}\n```\n\n### Dynamic descriptors\n\nDynamic descriptors are typically composed of a name and phone number or URL. The name must include the business name, followed by a product name or identifier, separated by an asterisk (*). Depending on the type of transaction you're creating, the length/character limits may differ from those outlined above. For example, you can only specify up to 18 characters for dynamic descriptor names on Braintree Marketplace transactions. See below for details on[Venmo](#venmo),[PayPal](#paypal), and[Braintree Marketplace](#braintree-marketplace)dynamic descriptors.\n\nYour processor may also restrict which descriptor values you can pass; certain processors allow you to pass URLs instead of phone numbers, while others accept only phone numbers or only names. If your processor supports URLs and you send both a phone number and URL, we will only pass the URL to the processor.[Contact us](/braintree/help?issue=updateDescriptor)for more information on your processor's specific requirements.\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :amount =\u003e \"10.00\",\n    :payment_method_nonce =\u003e nonce_from_the_client,\n    :descriptor =\u003e {\n        :name =\u003e \"company*my product\",\n        :phone =\u003e \"3125551212\",\n        :url =\u003e \"company.com\"\n    }\n)\n\u003ca href=\"http://result.transaction.descriptor.name\"\u003eresult.transaction.descriptor.name\u003c/a\u003e //=\u003e \"company*my product\"\nresult.transaction.descriptor.phone //=\u003e \"3125551212\"\n```\n\n#### Venmo\n\nVenmo only supports the dynamic descriptorname. Its format allows alpha-numeric characters and+-.(space included); any other characters will result in the dynamic descriptor name not being included in the full descriptor sent to the processor.\n\nThe full descriptor submitted to the processor is structured as follows:\n\n\n- The default prefix ofVENMO *(Two whitespaces).\n- TheBusiness Namesubmitted in the[Venmo application form](/braintree/articles/guides/payment-methods/venmo#go-live).\n- TheDynamic Descriptor Namesubmitted in the[transaction.sale()](#descriptor-name)or[transaction.submit_for_settlement()](/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/submit-for-settlement/ruby#descriptor)call.\n\nAn example of a full descriptor with a valid dynamic descriptor name is: VENMO *AStore O-1234, whereAStoreis theBusiness NameandO-1234is theDynamic Descriptor Name. If the dynamic descriptor name contains invalid characters, e.g. 0#1234, the entire dynamic descriptor name will be ignored.\n**NOTE**\nThe full descriptor is limited to 22 characters. If this limit is exceeded, the Business Name and Dynamic Descriptor Name portion will be truncated as needed. If you want to change the Business Name of the descriptor, you can edit your Venmo profile via the Venmo Processing page in the Control Panel. This will also update the name displayed to customers in the Venmo app during transaction processing.\n\n\n#### PayPal\n\nFor PayPal transactions only, the dynamic descriptor is limited to a total of 22 characters and includes the following elements:\n\n\n- The default prefix ofPAYPAL *\n- Your PayPal hard descriptor*\n- The product portion of yourname\n\nThese rules apply only when the payment method is PayPal. Card and other payment methods follow their own descriptor rules.\n\n*Depending on your PayPal account setup, the PayPal hard descriptor may not be included in the dynamic descriptor. You can update the hard descriptor value from your[PayPal console](https://www.paypal.com/login).\n\nThey`name`must meet the following guidelines:\n\n\n- Must include your registered Doing Business As (DBA) name, followed by an asterisk and a product description\n- The DBA portion must be 3, 7 or 12 characters long - this portion will be dropped from your dynamic descriptor\n\n\n**NOTE**\nIf the three parts of your dynamic descriptor combined exceed the 22 character limit, the `name` portion will automatically be truncated as needed.\n\nThe payment information displayed to a customer in their PayPal account overview does not contain the dynamic descriptor. The information displayed there is data the merchant has configured with PayPal directly (e.g. business name, email address, business contact details).\n#### Braintree Marketplace\n\nThe only dynamic descriptor value we will pass for Braintree Marketplace transactions is the`name`you specify. We will not send any dynamic`phone`or`url`values to the processor, but we will pass the`phone`from the hard descriptor on your master merchant account.\n\nThe dynamic descriptor name can only contain the ASCII characters a-z, A-Z, the numbers 0-9, and the characters.-+and spaces (it can't contain special characters like,, and). The maximum length is 18 characters; we will truncate any longer strings. The descriptor we pass to the processor will start with\"BT *\", followed by the`name`you specify.\n\n\n- If the specified name is 12 characters or fewer, the descriptor we pass to the processor will end with a randomly generated 6-character string (e.g.123abc) which identifies the sub-merchant:\n### \n```html\nBT *MYDESCRIPTOR123abc\n```\n\n- If the specified name is 13 characters or greater, the descriptor we pass to the processor will not end with a randomly generated 6-character string:\n### \n```html\nBT *MYDESCRIPTORISLONG\n```\n\n\n\n**NOTE**\nThe sub-merchant can't access the 6-character stringwe automatically append it to the descriptor name after you submit the transaction request. The string can't be changed, as it is required in order to identify each transaction we process for the sub-merchant.\n\n\n### Hold a Braintree Marketplace transaction in escrow on creation\n\nUpon creating a[Braintree Marketplace transaction](/braintree/docs/guides/braintree-marketplace/create), you can specify that its funds should be held in escrow. These funds can then be[released](/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/release-from-escrow)at your discretion. By default, funds are not held in escrow.\n### Ruby\n```ruby\nresult = gateway.transaction.sale(\n    :amount =\u003e \"100.00\",\n    :merchant_account_id =\u003e \"blue_ladders_store\",\n    :payment_method_nonce =\u003e nonce_from_the_client,\n    :options =\u003e {\n        :submit_for_settlement =\u003e true,\n        :hold_in_escrow =\u003e true\n    },\n    :service_fee_amount =\u003e \"10.00\"\n)\n```\n"},"routes/braintree/docs":null},"actionData":null,"errors":null},"future":{"v2_dev":true,"unstable_postcss":false,"unstable_tailwind":false,"v2_errorBoundary":false,"v2_headers":false,"v2_meta":true,"v2_normalizeFormMethod":false,"v2_routeConvention":false}};</script><script nonce="zv28CUFzPh52Y8Co9Y+R9EBxeQ/OS2qg9BrvOMB67Tpk56uA" type="module" async="">import "https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/manifest-D829D641.js";
